Japanese Government Establishes Raw Silk Visiting Bureau in the United States 168

To Promote Japanese Silk Sales in the United States

The United States is the largest silk consuming country in the world, requiring 600,000 dan of raw silk annually. Although affected by the recession last year, it still consumed 553,888 dan of raw silk. Japan supplied 518,794 dan, accounting for 90% of the US sales. However, the Japanese government still believes it is insufficient. According to Miao Zhongxiu, director of the Raw Silk Inspection Department of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, he received a letter from Tao Di, director of the New York Raw Silk Inspection Institute, reporting that the Japanese government recently sent Yoshida, former director of the Yokohama Raw Silk Inspection Institute, and Shiga, former representative of the Japan Silk Industry Association in the United States, to the United States to organize the Japanese Raw Silk Visiting Bureau in the United States to promote Japanese silk sales in the United States. It also prepared one million Japanese yen to conduct propaganda work for Japanese silk in order to enhance Japanese-American silk trade relations. The American silk industry believes that this move is very important. Tao Di sent a letter asking China to catch up quickly and not fall behind. According to Mr. Miao, regarding China's liaison with the American silk industry, he plans to discuss concrete measures with He Bingxian, director of the International Trade Bureau, in the near future and proceed with them effectively.

The Industrial and Railway Exhibition held by Jiaotong University in Shanghai has closed on the 9th. Chai-Pan Lawsuit Proceeds to Settlement 171

The lawsuit between Chai Yanxu and his uncle Pan Xiangsheng and cousin Ji Zhongren, regarding the misappropriation of a large sum of property entrusted to them, was again due for further hearing yesterday. The plaintiff Chai Yanxu and witness Lou Mingshi were both present, while the defendant was only represented by lawyer Chen Tingrui. Lawyer Chen stated that the two parties are close relatives and the defendant is willing to settle with the plaintiff, requesting the court to postpone the hearing to facilitate the settlement. Lawyer Jiang, representing the plaintiff, stated that the defendant had sent someone to his law firm to negotiate a settlement. The plaintiff, in order to settle the matter peacefully, agreed to the settlement and requested the court to grant a postponement. Finally, Judge Zhan, after reviewing the matter, ordered that the case be postponed for two weeks. If the settlement is unsuccessful during the postponement, the court will reconvene for further hearing.

Four Banks Preparation Vault Issues Preparation Report 174

171st Time

The Four Banks Preparation Vault is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu banks and specializes in issuing banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. According to the vault's issuance regulations, the issuance of banknotes must be fully backed by reserves, with a minimum cash reserve of 60% and a maximum guarantee reserve of 40%. The announcement is made once a week and is reviewed by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The following is a copy of the 171st announcement of the Shanghai Preparation Vault on April 8, 1933: Amount of banknotes in circulation: 18,739,037 yuan. The Special Features of Guanshengyuan's Ming Shrimp The Ming shrimp after the Qingming Festival is full of roe and oil, and its meat is fat and tender, with a special flavor that is different from ordinary products. The Guanshengyuan catering department in Shanghai is famous for making seasonal dishes, and it is especially skilled in cooking Ming shrimp. It is said that before making it, the green line in the back of the Ming shrimp is removed because the line is quite bitter and not suitable for eating. Then, it is fried with shrimp paste produced in Zhongshan County. Its taste is delicious and different from what is made in ordinary restaurants. Therefore, those who visit in recent days like to eat it, and the demand is greater than the supply.

He is proficient in internal medicine, surgery, obstetrics, and gynecology. Those who seek his treatment are always successful. He is especially kind and attentive to poor patients and people in the education and journalism fields, and he treats them carefully. He does not have the bad habit of Western doctors who are always calculating their fees. His diagnosis is meticulous and his prescriptions are cautious. On the 10th of this month, she accidentally swallowed a peanut, which went deep into her trachea. She coughed and choked continuously. Dr. Li Guo, director of the Otolaryngology Department of the hospital, was urgently called for consultation and performed surgery immediately. The peanut was removed within a few minutes, turning the danger into safety and celebrating a new life. The skill is amazing. In addition to serving at the hospital, Dr. Li also has a clinic at No. 1205 Jing'an Temple Road. He is available for consultation there every afternoon. 20th Anniversary Publication of the Chemical Industry Society: The China Chemical Industry Society has been established for more than 20 years. The company had planned to edit a special commemorative publication two years ago for its 20th anniversary. However, due to the January 28th Incident, most of the manuscripts were lost, so the publication was delayed. Recently, due to the urging of various circles, who have been sending letters and requesting copies, the company has slightly reorganized the remaining manuscripts and sent them to the printers. The publication has now been published. The entire book uses domestic Tianzhang Daolin paper and is exquisitely printed by the Hanwen Zhengxing Printing Bureau, with clear fonts and beautiful typesetting. The content includes Fang Yexian's "An Overview of the Cosmetics Industry," Hong Shaoyi's "China's Seasoning Industry," Wu Deming's "Investigation of the Japanese Pyrethrum Industry," and more than thirty articles, including essays, literary works, anecdotes, and novels, as well as more than twenty photographic illustrations. The entire book is a beautifully bound volume and is not for sale. If domestic product organizations, industrial and commercial institutions, and chambers of commerce, etc., send letters requesting a copy, one will be presented free of charge.

Reader's Advice

A Collection of Letters Discussing the Question "Can We Return to the Countryside?" (5): Mr. Zhu Tianqing from Benhang Writes: Sympathizing with Mr. You Huaigao's Method 181

After reading Mr. Liu Simin's "Discussion on 'Can We Return to the Countryside?'" today, I feel that Mr. Liu has some misunderstandings about Mr. You's views, so I am not afraid to show my ignorance and write this article specifically to point out Mr. Liu's misunderstandings. (1) Mr. You said: "People who have lived in the city for a long time may feel the boredom of loneliness, but I feel that in this time of national crisis, seeing the decadent life in the city, it is better to find a quiet and lovely village to seek another way out, and use ten years of my ability to build a 'new type of Peach Blossom Spring' that I have imagined." These words are truly insightful and have a very profound vision. Of course, people who have lived in the city for a long time often feel the troubles of life. If they have the opportunity to go to the countryside, they can not only get a kind of adjustment in their lives, but also benefit their body and mind. As for Xiongshengjun, instead of feeling the difficulties of a stagnant life in the city, it is easier to solve life in the countryside. In this way, naturally, Xiongshengjun needs to return to the countryside. Furthermore, everyone knows that rural education in our country is underdeveloped. Because of the underdevelopment of rural education, the average farmer does not know how to improve cultivation, and is extremely negligent when it comes to national affairs. To be honest, if rural education in China were developed, then China's agriculture would have flourished long ago, and would not be as sluggish as it is now. Although the bankruptcy of agriculture is due to internal strife, if one wants to do a good job, one must first sharpen one's tools. The increase in production volume still depends on the improvement of utensils. The improvement of utensils, of course, depends on the farmers who are on the scene. However, farmers who are ignorant and unknowing, farmers who have not received education, only know how to stick to the old ways. How can they know how to improve utensils, seeds, etc.? Why do farmers in Europe and the United States know how to improve utensils and seeds, while farmers in our country do not? This is of course due to lack of knowledge, so lack of knowledge is obviously due to the underdevelopment of rural education. Here, we can see the importance of rural education. Therefore, Mr. You teaching Xiongshengjun to return to the countryside not only allows Xiongshengjun to adjust his body and mind, but also makes life easier to solve. At the same time, he can devote Xiongshengjun's strength to the development of rural education, which is not without benefit to the country. Why not do it with one stroke and three gains? If Siminjun does not teach Xiongshengjun to go back, may I ask, is there another way out? Otherwise, call Xiongshengjun to wander in a foreign land and starve to death? As for finding another profession, to be honest, in Shanghai, where supply exceeds demand, Xiongshengjun may not be able to find a foothold for a while! (2) The "new type of Peach Blossom Spring" is a kind of imagined construction. The Japanese invasion and the communist disturbance are a kind of destruction. Each tends to extremes. If you are afraid of destruction, then don't build. However, destruction is destruction, and construction is still necessary. People in the world know that war is destructive, and they predict that war is inevitable. In order to avoid war and destruction of construction, they should not engage in construction, but the opposite is true. Looking around the world, which country does not strive to engage in construction? If Siminjun looked at it, they must be crazy, but they are not crazy! 丨丨 Then why is this? Hey! Hey! This means that construction is construction, and destruction is destruction. If you build a "new type of Peach Blossom Spring" and are afraid of the destruction of Japan and communism, it is like a person who is afraid of death after being born. If people are afraid of death, it is better not to be born. I said, Siminjun, if you are afraid of death, it is better not to be born. Furthermore, Mr. You's so-called construction of a "new type of imagined Peach Blossom Spring" does not mean that after building the "new type of Peach Blossom Spring," he can ignore national affairs, "regardless of the Zhou and Qin dynasties, let alone the Republic of China." It is well known that the main point of building a "new type of Peach Blossom Spring" is to make people aware of national affairs, because the starting point of building a "new type of Peach Blossom Spring" is to develop rural education, so the highest purpose of developing rural education is to make people understand national affairs. In short, this "new type of Peach Blossom Spring" is not the "Peach Blossom Spring" in Tao Qian's imagined world that does not ask about worldly affairs. Siminjun has not yet seen through this point and added criticism, which can be said to be extremely ridiculous. (3) The bankruptcy of the countryside is not only because the countryside is dominated by the city. It is well known that the bankruptcy of the countryside is complex, and each has its own advantages and disadvantages. For example, the bankruptcy of the Chinese countryside is due to internal strife and the constant disturbances of the communists. However, if rural education in China were developed, then the bankruptcy of the countryside would not be a complete failure. Indeed, rural education in the United States and Japan is ten or a hundred times better than ours. However, Siminjun, may I ask, is the extent of the bankruptcy of rural areas in the United States and Japan more severe than in our country? If my observation is correct, then I think it may not be! (4) Furthermore, generally speaking, people in the city are indeed much more cunning than people in the countryside. If you don't believe me, just look at the darkness in Shanghai. May I ask, is there any in the countryside? Siminjun, you said, "Most of the 3.2 million people in Shanghai (shop assistants, workers, and some young students) are still honest and not deceitful." This may not be entirely true. You must know that nothing in the world is absolute. You say that iron is cold, but it can also be hot when exposed to the sun or in the fire. You say that shop assistants, workers, and some young students are still honest and not deceitful is unreliable, because shop assistants, workers, and students also have good and bad differences!

Military Training to Continue in Secondary and Higher Schools This Summer 183

—A Total of Three Weeks—

Nanjing, December 12th: The Ministry of Education has approved the Training Supervisory Department's notification to all education bureaus, instructing public and private high schools and above to continue to implement three weeks of strict military training this summer, and stipulates the following class hours: 1. The minimum academic and practical class time per week must be 24 hours. 2. How should the academic one-third and practical two-thirds be allocated? The military instructor should discuss with the school principal and make a proper plan, and report it for verification before May of this year.

Political News from the Ministry of Education 184

The Ministry of Education's recent political news for the past week is summarized below: (1) Instructed the Jiangsu Education Department that the request to reform the three-year system of county normal schools to a four-year system should be approved. (2) Instructed the Guangdong Education Department that the order to reform the school system decided by the Southwest Education Reform Committee should be temporarily suspended. (3) The Jiangxi Education Department reported that Jiangxi Middle School was ordered to suspend operations within a time limit for improper management, which was approved for record. (4) The Shanxi Education Department reported that Shangzhi Girls' Middle School would postpone the establishment of junior high school from this year, which was approved for record. (5) The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau reported four regulations on graduation joint examinations for primary and secondary schools, which were approved for record. (6) Replied to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that at the Fifth International Administrative Science Conference, it was requested to consult with the chargé d'affaires in Austria to represent the meeting nearby. (7) Instructed the Beiping Municipal Social Bureau to report that Hongda Middle School requested to change the four-two system to a three-three system, which was approved for record.

Fujian Education Department Issues Scholarships to Poor Students 185

Nine Students Including Zheng Chunting Were Selected and Admitted

To Be Issued After Enrollment in the Summer

In order to subsidize poor high school students in the province to enter higher education and university students to continue their studies, the Fujian Rescue Education Department held a scholarship for poor students. After examination and review, more than 80 students were approved to participate in the examination, which was held in Fuzhou, Shanghai, Beiping, and Wuchang. Except for the Fuzhou District, which was directly handled by the Education Department, the other districts were entrusted to local education institutions to conduct the examination. However, the test questions for each subject were all formulated separately by the examination committee hired by the department, sealed and sent to the examination institutions in each district. All test papers were sealed, and the test papers of students in districts outside the province were sent back to the Education Department, where the original question setters were invited to review them in the department to show prudence. It was found that 37 students who did not go to higher education and 27 students who went to higher education participated in the examination. The "Scholarship Committee for Poor Students and University Scholarships" carefully calculated and decided the number of places to be admitted for each subject. It was found that the original examination was scheduled to select two students each in liberal arts, engineering, science, medicine, and agriculture. However, the results of the examination showed that the performance in agriculture was poor, so it was finally decided to select one more student each in liberal arts and science to make up for the shortage in agriculture. As for the students who applied for engineering and passed, there was only one. In order to cultivate specialized engineering talents, the Education Department specially set up two backup places to show encouragement. A total of nine students were selected for the liberal arts, science, engineering, and medical fields, and two backup students, Ji Zuxuan and Liu Yongmao, were selected for engineering. The committee decided that Li Zuxuan should apply for the engineering department of the university within this summer vacation. If he can be admitted, he will be given a scholarship. If he is not admitted, Liu Yongmao will be used to fill the vacancy. The list of students who have been officially admitted is as follows: Liberal Arts: Zheng Tingchun, from Yongtai, graduated from Gezhi; Gao Mingkai, from Pingtan, graduated from Yinghua; Lin Enqing, from Minhou, graduated from Yinghua; Science: Lin Renmu, from Minhou, graduated from the science department; Lin Kongxiang, from Minhou, graduated from Jimei; Guo Dongbing, from Nan'an, graduated from the Xiamen University Affiliated High School; Engineering: You Dezi, from Minhou, graduated from Fuzhou High School; Medical: Lu Songci, from Gutian, graduated from Yinghua; Ye Xingjie, from Minhou, graduated from Yinghua.

County Normal Schools in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province Changed to a Four-Year System 186

School Names Changed to Simple Normal Schools

The Jiangsu Education Department convened a meeting of education directors from various counties last year. The Feng County Education Bureau proposed to change the three-year system of county normal schools to a four-year system. The conference decided to submit it to the Education Department for submission to the Ministry of Education for review. The chairman of the conference, Xu Mu and Du Yijian, immediately submitted the resolution to the Education Department for review. After receiving the submission from the Education Department, it was submitted to the Ministry of Education. The Ministry of Education then issued an instruction, saying that the request to change the three-year system of county normal schools to a four-year system was not inconsistent with the provisions of Article 124 of Chapter 15 of the recently promulgated regulations on normal schools, and should be approved. However, the school name should be changed to a certain county's simple normal school in accordance with the regulations on normal schools. The Education Department has instructed Shanghai, Gaochun, Huaiyin, Xiaoxian, Changshan, Pixian, Suqian, Muyang, Ganyu, Suining, and other counties with county normal schools or middle schools to comply.

Ministry Order on Matters Needing Attention in the Implementation of Regulations on Teachers in Primary and Secondary Schools 187

Provincial and Municipal Education Departments and Bureaus Shall Handle and Report Together Before July of This Year

The Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating that the Primary School Law, the Middle School Law, the Normal School Law, and the Vocational School Law were previously promulgated by the National Government and issued by the Ministry. Now, the Ministry has formulated the Primary School Regulations, the Middle School Regulations, the Normal School Regulations, and the Vocational School Regulations in accordance with the laws, regarding the establishment, management, funding, staffing, curriculum, training, equipment, performance examination, academic year, semester, holiday dates, micro-charges, and the appointment of teachers and school administration. All items have been carefully formulated. In the future, primary and secondary normal schools and vocational schools in various places must comply.

According to these regulations, the education administrative organs of various provinces and cities should refer to the local situation and formulate separate regulations and measures. The departments should check and stipulate separately. Also, the existing schools of various types in various places that need to change their establishment and correct their names, and the principals of various schools who still have concurrent positions, should appoint full-time principals from August 1, 1933. The departments should plan and order compliance, and list the special matters that should be noted when implementing these four regulations in various provinces and cities, and report them together for review before July of this year.

(1) Regarding Primary Schools 188

(1) In provinces and cities where there are still separately established senior primary schools, junior primary schools should be added or merged with other local junior primary schools in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the Primary School Regulations.

(2) There is no unified method for naming primary schools. In the future, the affiliated schools should be instructed to comply with the provisions of Article 11 of the Primary School Regulations and quickly correct the school names to show uniformity.

(3) Primary schools specially established by various institutions other than education administrative organs are under the jurisdiction of the institutions and are not subject to the supervision and guidance of the local education administrative organs in charge, which is detrimental to the unity of education administration. The education administrative organs should comply with the provisions of Article 14 of the Primary School Regulations and be responsible for the supervision and guidance of such schools.

(4) If the department has established experimental schools, each school should be instructed to report the experimental plan and results to the competent education administrative organ for submission to the Ministry for approval and record in accordance with the provisions of Article 17 of the Primary School Regulations. Primary schools that are not experimental in nature and use the name of experimental schools should change their names uniformly.

(5) The standard for primary school funding, the method for public review of primary school funding, the method for calculating the scores of primary school children in each subject, the method for examining moral character and physical education, the method for children's promotion and demotion, and the salary scale of primary school teachers and staff and the method for annual salary increase should be formulated separately by the department in accordance with the provisions of Article 22, Article 23, Article 53, and Article 89 of the Primary School Regulations and submitted to the Ministry for approval and record.

(6) There is no standard for primary school fees. The affiliated schools should be strictly ordered to make corrections in accordance with Chapter 11 of the Primary School Regulations.

(7) There are not many primary school education research organizations in various provinces and cities. Even if there are such organizations, they all act independently and have no system. Various research associations should be organized in accordance with the provisions of Chapter 13 of the Primary School Regulations, and the organizational regulations of the research associations should be formulated and submitted to the Ministry for record.

(2) Regarding Middle Schools 189

(1) If the public or private junior high schools or senior high schools in various places are established separately, they shall be prefixed with the words "junior" or "senior" respectively in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the Middle School Regulations. The names of each school shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the Regulations. If the names of the public and private middle schools under the jurisdiction of the provinces and cities do not comply with these provisions, they shall be ordered to correct them uniformly from the 22nd academic year, and the corrected names shall be reported to the Ministry for record before the summer vacation of this year. (2) Normal schools shall be established independently. If the provinces, cities, and counties are limited by funding and cannot establish them separately for a while, simple normal departments and special normal departments may be established separately in public junior high schools and senior high schools, but they must comply with the provisions of Article 8 of the Middle School Regulations.

(3) The matters reported by the public and private middle schools in various places are not uniform, and there are many omissions. In the future, the matters that should be reported on schedule and the reports of school inspectors should be reported to the Ministry in accordance with the provisions of Article 9, Article 10, Article 12, and Article 13 of the Middle School Regulations, and no omissions are allowed.

(4) The percentage of distribution of recurrent expenses of middle schools in various provinces and cities shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 17 of the Middle School Regulations, and the method for auditing the income and expenditure of public and private middle school funds shall be formulated in accordance with Article 18 of the Regulations and submitted to the Ministry for record.

(5) The standard for public funding to subsidize private middle schools in counties shall be stipulated by the departments and bureaus and submitted to the Ministry for review.

(6) Middle schools that set up vocational subjects shall first submit the subjects and equipment status to the Ministry for review.

(7) The methods for training management and rewards and punishments for middle school students shall be formulated by the departments and bureaus in accordance with the provisions of Article 42 of the Middle School Regulations, and submitted to the Ministry for approval and implementation. The method for calculating academic performance shall also be formulated by the departments and bureaus in accordance with the provisions of Article 67 of the Regulations and submitted to the Ministry for review.

(8) Each province shall designate a location and select several suitable provincial middle schools to concurrently run spring semester classes, and submit the names of the designated schools to the Ministry for record. (9) Each province and city shall consider the local situation and stipulate the proportion of new students with equivalent academic ability accepted by the middle schools under its jurisdiction, and submit it to the Ministry for record.

(10) There is no definite standard for the fees currently charged to students in middle schools in various provinces and cities, and the fees charged by private schools are particularly high, making it difficult for students to bear. They shall be stipulated separately in accordance with the provisions of Article 86 of the Middle School Regulations and submitted to the Ministry for record. The tuition fees collected in public schools shall be submitted to the national, provincial, municipal, and county treasuries separately in accordance with the provisions of Article 82 of the Regulations. The library fees and sports fees shall be handled separately by public and private middle schools in accordance with the provisions of Article 82 and Article 83 of the Regulations.

(11) The method for scholarships for provincial and municipal middle schools shall be formulated by the departments and bureaus, and the amount of scholarships for county and private schools shall be stipulated separately by the departments and bureaus in accordance with the regulations of each county and school, and shall be submitted to the Ministry for record.

(12) The appointment of principals and teachers in middle schools in various places must strictly comply with the qualifications and appointment procedures stipulated in the various articles of the Middle School Regulations. The teachers are appointed for an initial term and a renewed term. When the original teachers of each school continue to be employed in the next semester, it will be a renewal. After the qualifications of the teachers in each middle school have been verified by the education administrative organs of the province and city, and the appointment letter is sent in the name of the school, if the principal changes midway, the teachers will not advance or retreat with the principal.

(13) The staff of middle schools in various places must not be additionally established in accordance with the provisions of Articles 102, 103, and 104 of the Middle School Regulations. (14) Each province and city shall formulate measures for the further study of middle school teachers and submit them to the Ministry for approval and implementation.

(15) The salary scale for teachers in provincial, municipal, and county middle schools and the method for annual salary increase shall be stipulated by the departments and bureaus in accordance with the provisions of Article 116 of the Middle School Regulations and submitted to the Ministry for review.

(III) Regarding Normal Schools 190

(I) Normal schools should be established independently. The normal school departments originally established within provincial and municipal middle schools should be separated and changed into normal schools starting from the next academic year. Each province should also, in accordance with Article 10 of the Normal School Regulations, divide the entire province into several normal school districts and establish normal schools and women's normal schools separately. If, due to financial constraints, the original normal school departments within middle schools cannot be fully separated and established immediately, special normal departments and simplified normal departments may be established separately within public senior or junior middle schools in accordance with Articles 3 and 6 of the Normal School Regulations. Overall, careful planning should be done and implemented starting from the next academic year.

(II) Private normal schools in various regions, except for those that are kindergarten normal departments and those for training elementary school specialized teachers in subjects such as crafts, home economics, drawing, music, and physical education, and have already been registered with the Ministry or with the educational administrative organs of various provinces and cities, are allowed to continue operating. All others should be ordered to be converted into vocational schools or middle schools starting from the next academic year. Furthermore, starting from the 22nd year of the Republic, requests from individuals to establish any private normal school will not be permitted.

(III) Provincial and municipal departments should, within possible limits, and considering local conditions,

move most normal schools to rural areas.

(IV) The naming of normal schools established in various provinces and cities is inconsistent and should be corrected separately in accordance with the provisions of Article 11 of the Normal School Regulations. A list of all normal schools under their jurisdiction and the corrected names must be reported before the summer vacation of this year, and the changes should be uniformly implemented starting from the next academic year.

(V) The reporting of matters by normal schools in various provinces and cities is inconsistent, and many omissions are not reported. Hereafter, the provisions of Articles 12, 13, and 15 of the Normal School Regulations should be strictly followed, and reports should be filled out accurately and on time.

(VI) The expenditure of funds for normal schools in various provinces and cities has consistently lacked reasonable allocation, which greatly affects educational efficiency. Starting from the next academic year, the allocation of recurring expenses for each normal school should strictly follow the percentage specified in Article 20 of the Normal School Regulations. Furthermore, the respective departments and bureaus should, in accordance with Article 21 of the Regulations, formulate methods for auditing the income and expenditure of normal school funds and submit them to the Ministry for record.

(VII) The standards for provincial subsidies to county-run normal schools should be stipulated by the respective departments and submitted to the Ministry for record.

(VIII) The curriculum standards for normal schools in various provinces and cities shall temporarily continue to apply the Provisional Standards for Senior High School Normal Department Curriculum promulgated by the Ministry. Rural normal schools should add courses related to rural areas and agriculture. Teachers of each subject should compile their own teaching materials and submit them to the Ministry for record in accordance with the provisions of Article 31 of the Normal School Regulations.

(IX) Each province and city should designate one or two provincial or municipal normal schools to, in addition to implementing general training, establish specialized subject groups to train specialized elementary school teachers. The designated schools and the methods for studying specialized subjects in groups should be submitted to the Ministry for record.

(X) Each province and city should stipulate measures for student training management, rewards, and punishments in normal schools and submit them to the Ministry for approval.

(XI) Each province and city should stipulate measures for setting up scholarship awards in normal schools and submit them to the Ministry for approval and implementation.

(XII) The appointment of principals and teachers in normal schools in various regions must henceforth strictly follow the qualifications and appointment procedures stipulated in the various articles of Chapter 13 of the Normal School Regulations. The terms of teachers are divided into initial appointment and formal appointment. When the original teachers of each school continue to be employed in the next academic year, it shall be considered a renewed appointment. Once the qualifications of teachers in each normal school have been reviewed by the provincial and municipal educational administrative organs, and the appointment letter is issued in the name of the school, if the principal changes midway, the teachers will not advance or retreat along with the principal.

(XIII) The staff of each normal school must follow the provisions of Articles 103, 104, and 105 of the Normal School Regulations and must not be increased beyond the stipulated number.

(XIV) Each province and city should formulate measures for the continuing education of normal school teachers and submit them to the Ministry for approval and implementation.

(XV) The salary scale and annual increment system for teachers in provincial, municipal, and county-run normal schools should be stipulated by the respective departments and bureaus in accordance with the provisions of Article 115 of the Normal School Regulations and submitted to the Ministry for record.

(IV) Regarding Vocational Schools 191

(I) Vocational schools should be established independently. Various vocational departments originally established within provincial and municipal middle schools should, starting from the next academic year, consider the circumstances and transfer students other than those in vocational departments to other middle schools and convert the original schools into vocational schools.

(II) The establishment of departments in vocational schools has lacked uniform standards, with arbitrary establishments and simple scales, which affects the progress of students' studies. Hereafter, the provisions of Article 8 of the Regulations must be followed.

(III) The naming of vocational schools has lacked a fixed method. Hereafter, the provisions of Article 5 of the Regulations must be followed.

(IV) Each county and city must establish junior vocational schools as much as possible. Before they are established, the provisions of Article 11 of the Regulations must be followed.

(V) Each province, city, and county should encourage private individuals, organizations, factories, stores, farms, and other vocational institutions to establish vocational schools, and provide appropriate subsidies in accordance with the provisions of Article 21 of the Regulations.

(VI) In the time allocation of vocational school curricula, practical training should, as a principle, account for at least half.

(VII) The content of vocational school practical training venues must be substantial, and the appropriate methods should be adopted in accordance with the provisions of Article 39 of the Regulations, taking into account the actual situation.

(VIII) Vocational school funding cannot be equal to that of ordinary secondary schools and must be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 19 of the Regulations.

(IX) The length of study for each level of vocational school should be determined according to the nature of the departments offered.

(X) The training environment of vocational schools should strive to be consistent with the students' future actual vocational environment, paying attention to students' vocational knowledge and skills, vocational ethics, civic training, physical exercise, work habits, etc., and cultivating their production knowledge and skills.

(XI) Vocational school assignments should focus on practicality.

(XII) Vocational schools should earnestly follow the provisions of Article 69 of the Regulations, contact vocational institutions, organize vocational placement departments, and provide guidance at any time to graduates who encounter difficulties after employment.

(XIII) The tuition fees and practical material fees of vocational schools have often been arbitrarily collected. Hereafter, the provisions of Articles 67 and 68 of the Regulations should be strictly followed.

(XIV) If vocational schools need to implement vacation assignments due to practical needs, they should implement them in accordance with Articles 64, 65, and 66 of the Regulations. The educational administrative organs of each province and city should, with reference to local conditions, formulate implementation measures and submit them to the Ministry for record and implementation.

(XV) Vocational schools must pay attention to skills and experience when hiring teachers and may consider hiring technicians from the vocational world.

The team was announced and ordered to be distributed. In addition, the regulations of primary and secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools must be promulgated. The hall must comply and order the subordinates to comply. From the date of implementation of the regulations of primary and secondary schools, the temporary regulations of primary and secondary schools announced by the former university institute will be repealed. This order is to distribute regulations of primary and secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Zhirenyong Affiliated Elementary School to Replace Principal 194

Investigation Form for Private Elementary Schools Not Yet Submitted

Must Comply Within One Week or Registration Will Be Revoked

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued a directive to the board of directors of the private Zhirenyong Girls' Middle School Affiliated Elementary School yesterday, stating that the Private Elementary School Overview Investigation Form for the first semester of the 21st year of the Republic was issued to various private elementary schools for completion and submission last year. An investigation found that all schools have complied and submitted the form to the bureau, except for the affiliated elementary school, which has repeatedly been urged to submit the form but has not yet done so, which is a deliberate violation of regulations and an intentional disregard for orders. The bureau affairs meeting has resolved to order the school's board of directors to replace the principal and submit the form to the bureau within one week of receiving this document. If the school fails to comply, its registration will be immediately revoked and its registration certificate will be canceled. This directive is issued to the school's board of directors for compliance, and the handling of the matter must be reported.

Jinan Wins Over Fuzhong (Women's) 199

Jinan Fouls Points ▲Fuzhong Fouls Points

Amateur Grade A Billiards

Bernal's Performance Was Excellent at the Start of the Second Week Yesterday 204

Defeating Maxwell Was as Easy as Turning His Hand

The Result: 1,000 Points to 548

—Schedule Changes, No Competition Today—

British master Bernal performed exceptionally well in the second week of Shanghai's amateur Grade A billiards competition yesterday. All the spectators in the audience were amazed. Bernal has a long-standing relationship with Shanghai's billiards community, at least for more than ten years. He also once ascended the league and held the reins. In recent years, Shanghai-Portuguese experts Li Gongying and Medina have appeared one after another, and the old general had to retire from the road of talent. Until recently, the edge has gradually emerged. Judging from yesterday's results, he has a tendency to restore his dominance. In the future, there will be a shocking competition with Medina. Maxwell's performance yesterday was almost surrendered to the old general's gun style, and there was no way to develop. In the first half, the difference was still close, with Bernal scoring 500 points and Maxwell scoring 340 points. In the second half, Bernal's bullets were all hits, and the gun was fired with a path. Whether it was self-falling, sending red, or opening a , everything was done as desired. At one point, there were three shots of 72, 54, 54, and other huge numbers. Far from this big difference, the final result was that Bernal won with 1,000 points against 548 points. Also, the order of the second week has been slightly changed. Parker vs. Medina in the first half has been changed to the 18th, Li Gongying vs. Xu Shizhang in the second half on the 19th, and Zhang Yingda vs. Shen Lince on the 20th.

Five Organization Track and Field Meet 205

Held at the American School on May 6th

China Youth, West Youth, Navy Youth, American School, and Mullins will hold a track and field meet at the American School on the afternoon of May 6th. Registration is from now until May 1st. Contact is Mr. Zhen of the Navy Youth Association. If the weather is not good at that time, it will be postponed to May 21st, and the registration period will also be extended to May 7th. The important officials, in addition to Westerners, are Wang Zhengting as the president and Shen Siliang as the chief referee. The program is as follows: Track events: (1) 100-yard preliminary round, two groups, take three people in each group, (2) one mile, (3) 100-yard final, (4) 400-yard final, (5) 220-yard preliminary round, two groups, take two people in each group, (6) low hurdles preliminary round, two groups, take three people in each group, (7) 880-yard final, (8) 220-yard final, (9) low hurdles final, (10) one-mile relay race. Field events: (1) 12-pound shot put, (2) triple jump, (3) discus, (4) long jump, (5) high jump, (6) pole vault. The scoring system is 5-3-2-1, and the relay race is doubled. Each organization may send three people to participate in one event.

All-China Games Preparatory Tai Chi Chuan Demonstration 206

Discussed with Various Primary and Secondary Schools in the Capital Yesterday

The Assembly Had 1,500 People Demonstrate

Nanjing, 12th. The All-China Games Preparatory Committee convened a joint meeting of principals of public and private primary and secondary schools in the capital on the 12th, chaired by Chu Minyi. Regarding the group performance of Tai Chi exercises during the Games, it was resolved: 1. 1,500 male and female students in grades four, five, and six of primary schools will be divided into several teams to participate in the performance. The uniforms will be in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education. Whether or not junior high schools should participate because their uniforms are inconsistent with those of primary schools will be discussed by the principals and the preparatory committee in a circular. 2. The training time will be set within the next week, and the preparatory committee will schedule physical education teachers from each school to start training in the auditorium of the Executive Yuan. First, Chu Minyi will hire Tai Chi experts to be in charge of training. After a considerable amount of time, they will go to each school to provide guidance, and then they will practice and perform several times in different districts. 3. The China Scout Association will be notified that primary schools will be performing Tai Chi exercises and will not participate in the Scout review. Regarding the singing of sports songs, it was resolved that the preparatory committee will first print 10,000 copies and distribute them to each school for practice through the Social Affairs Bureau. The number of participants will be determined separately. Regarding transportation matters, the Social Affairs Bureau will co-operate with the preparatory committee. Other hospitality matters will be handled by the preparatory committee.

Shenbao National Goods Weekly

Special Issue on Women and National Goods

Opening Remarks 210

— Pan Yang'an

Miss Xueying, covered in foreign goods, is extremely self-satisfied.

Entering and exiting social circles, utterly self-assured,

Flitting about like blooming branches, eyebrows dancing with delight;

Suddenly, she encounters a plain and simple country woman,

Whose needlework from head to toe is all self-made.

She spins her own yarn, weaves her own cloth,

And everything used in her home for food, clothing, shelter, and daily life is domestic.

Simple and rustic, yet she can represent Chinese housewives.

Modern girl, please stop laughing at her, stop disliking her,

Promoting foreign goods like you do, you truly don't understand the pain of national demise.

We have already changed our perspective, looking at these simple and honest women,

With much admiration and celebration.

Seeing you, so strangely adorned from head to toe in foreign goods,

We must consider you a complete "businesswoman," deserving of utmost disgust.

This is a humble little poem that I often unconsciously recite to many women, and they not only don't take offense but say it makes a lot of sense. Why not publish it in the National Products Weekly to contribute to the general public of housewives.

Young lady, when you get older and want to choose a suitable husband,

The first condition should be that he uses national products.

A talented man and beautiful woman, of course, are desirable,

But a complete playboy who only consumes foreign goods,

No matter how much your matchmaker tries, running east and west,

Because I love national products, I absolutely will not marry you, you conscienceless fool.

This is my second humble little poem, which I often unconsciously recite to many young girls, and they all nod and smile, urging me to publish it. Just as this journal is publishing a "Special Issue on Women and National Products," and needs an opening statement, since I don't have time to write an article, I'll just use this to fill the space.

A New Condition 211

— Bai Yu

丨Please Pay Attention, Ladies Who are About to Get Engaged丨

The evolution of the marriage system from "parents' orders and matchmaker's words" to the current system where the parties involved must agree can't be said as anything but a blessing for modern youth. One distinctive feature of the modern marriage system is that before engagement, whether a man or a woman, they all have several conditions for choosing a spouse in mind. There are many such conditions, such as personality, knowledge, ability, health, interests, appearance, economics, etc. Many experts spare no effort to conduct surveys and research. From what I have seen and heard in the conditions for choosing a spouse among modern youth, there is one point that has not been noticed. Readers, try to guess what condition it is. Since this article is published in the National Products Weekly, smart readers will naturally know it all: "The condition for choosing a spouse should include the condition of loving national products." That's right, my opinion is indeed so, that "loving national products" is a condition for choosing a spouse, and an important condition at that. Why? Let me explain.

The national crisis is so severe, and the people's livelihood is so impoverished. While promoting national products is not a miraculous cure for bringing the dead back to life, it can at least plug some leaks, cultivate some national wealth, and inflict some slight blows on our strong neighbors, seeking a glimmer of hope for the people's livelihood. To deny the value and necessity of promoting national products today is to be without blood and without conscience. However, there are many who say that national products should be promoted, but in reality, desperately act as voluntary promoters of foreign goods. Especially unmarried men, who consider using foreign goods to be fashionable, extravagant, and a display of their abundant economic capacity. But when you ask them whether national products should be promoted, they again wholeheartedly agree with promotion. People who contradict themselves in this way, their words are all false, all deceitful. If someone is like that regarding promoting national products, they are likely to be like that in all other matters. You see, they are full of professions of love for you, full of promises to be your slave, but all of it is false, all of it is deceitful. If someone had the courage to argue that national products should not be promoted, and then used foreign goods and consumed foreign goods, that kind of person would be a man who takes responsibility. But someone who admits that national products should be promoted, yet only seeks foreign goods, this is enough to prove their hypocrisy, prove their deceit. How dangerous it is to offer your virgin, pure heart to a hypocritical, deceitful man! A man who worships foreign goods, whether he buys foreign goods to show off, to follow fashion, or to flaunt them to you, his behavior is hateful, his heart is detestable. You must not be seduced by him, deceived by his dishonesty. Therefore, even when everything else about him meets your standards for choosing a spouse, you must also pay attention to whether he is a man who loves his country in word and deed, before deciding whether to follow him or not.

Truly loving and using national products can certainly prove that he is a genuine, patriotic man, and also that when forming a family in the future, many unnecessary wastes in the family's finances will be avoided. Your family will never experience economic hardship due to extravagance, nor will the family go bankrupt due to extravagance. At the same time, the national economy will not suffer losses because of your marriage. Ladies, this condition for choosing a spouse, its importance really doesn't fall behind conditions like personality, knowledge, ability, health, interests, appearance, economics, and so on.

Small Suggestions Regarding National Products 212

— Ms. Ai Cheng

I am a housewife from a middle-class family. My husband works in education, supporting the whole family with his salary. Our family of seven, I manage all the clothing for all four seasons. Whenever we buy new clothes, I spend quite a bit of effort on the fabrics. Children of course use national products, and even my husband and I like to use national products. But what are national products? What are foreign goods? It's not easy to tell. Sometimes I think it's a national product, and the store clerk also says it's a national product, but when I take it home and ask someone, they say it's a foreign product. All my happiness is doused with cold water, and there's no greater disappointment. Therefore, my first suggestion is that I hope the National Products Guidance Bureau or the China National Products Promotion Association can compile a national products guide to be my guide for buying national products in the future. National product colors are often not very fashionable, and the prices are more expensive than comparable foreign goods. For economic reasons, many women reluctantly buy foreign goods. Therefore, my second suggestion is that I hope national product manufacturers will research dyeing and manufacturing, and lower prices, adopting a policy of small profits and quick turnover. National product education should be deeply imprinted in children's minds; this is a responsibility that all housewives should bear. Not only should children be taught to use national products, but they should also be made to understand what national products are and why they should be used, cultivating good habits of using national products. This is the basic work of promoting national products. Therefore, my third suggestion is that I hope the national product industry will compile more pictures and stories about national products and give them away whenever women come to buy national products; this is the most effective advertising. The three suggestions above, although not very profound, are indeed easy to implement. People who are enthusiastic about promoting national products, it seems, should pay attention and study them.

Three Agreements 213

— Ms. Wanxia

Since men are so apathetic, I especially want to encourage our courage. If we are not yet married, we should propose an extremely important condition when engaged, three agreements, namely, neither of us will use foreign goods. If one party violates this, the other may propose divorce or punishment, all of which should be written clearly in the agreement.

If already married, then use stern admonition and close supervision.

As for everything used at home, it should be entirely up to us to purchase, without going through them. However, we must also carefully examine when purchasing, brands, factory names, raw materials, sources, and even inspect the manufacturing site when in doubt, so as not to be fooled, because there are many unscrupulous merchants.

If they accidentally buy a non-national product back, we will ruthlessly destroy this non-national product into pieces, or even cut off relations for two or three hours. This way, they will never do it again next time. However, you must be full of spirit, with the idea of ​​punishing one as a warning to a hundred, so that it is a permanent solution, otherwise, even if you quarrel every day, they will still violate the agreement every day. This kind of psychology must be understood.

A man will eventually be matched with a woman. A family cannot be formed without a woman. Isn't the heavy responsibility of promoting national products all on our shoulders? Conversely, destroying national products and promoting foreign goods is also our major sin.

Sisters, starting from today, quickly rise up to take on this extremely important responsibility of promoting national products, and never be criminals of the Republic of China.

Women's Only Responsibility in the National Crisis 215

— Zhu Wang Huanqing

"The merchant girl does not know the sorrow of a conquered nation, still singing 'Backyard Flowers' across the river." In the wine-green, lantern-red, gold-obsessed, and paper-drunk Shanghai, it seems like a time of singing and dancing, and although there are many patriots, what use are a few ordinary people with no money and no iron? However, the Republic of China ultimately belongs to the people, not to bureaucrats, politicians, local tyrants, and unscrupulous merchants, so we must not just watch and sigh, but each individual must earnestly start from themselves. Save on clothing and food, be diligent and hardworking, to be the backing of the Northeastern soldiers. Although it is said to be saving the country, it is actually saving ourselves. It is also to leave some room for future generations. As the saying goes, "If the skin is gone, what will the hair attach to?" May I ask, have the compatriots under the iron hooves felt the pain of national subjugation? We cannot hold steel knives and carry bombs to kill the Japanese invaders and recover the lost territories, but why are we not doing the easiest things, and instead learning to sing and dance in a leaky boat? How lamentable and pitiful! I believe that the only fundamental goal of saving the country is to improve families, educate children, and guide them onto the right path. If a housewife can manage her family well, in an orderly manner, educate her children to become sound citizens, and have no selfish or deceptive behavior, she can rectify any corrupt phenomena and influence her own children, relatives, friends, neighbors, servants, and maids to not buy foreign goods, let alone buy enemy goods. If a family still sees enemy goods being used there, we will despise their character and not associate with them. Because such people are fundamentally servile and can be said to be non-human. Let us women rise up quickly, improve families and educate children internally, and resist enemy goods and promote national products externally. This is our only fundamental responsibility for saving the country. Finally, let us shout a slogan:

"Women's only responsibility is to use national products."

Foreign goods are flooding the market, and women buy more of them than men. Among women, prostitutes who like to show off are especially prevalent. If we do not try to remedy this situation, profits will flow out, and the country and people will be impoverished as a result. Small newspapers cover news about women in brothels in more detail than larger newspapers. Your newspaper's second issue included an article titled "Swordsmen in Brothels," which shows that the Little Swordsman does not forget the brothels either. I hope that in the future, you will pay more attention to those in brothels who like to use national products and exclude foreign goods and publicize their actions. This will let decent women know that there are still patriotic compatriots in brothels who are enthusiastically using national products and rejecting foreign goods, and they may have a change of heart and switch to using national products. This may not be a bad way to promote national products. Your intentions are profound and admirable. Frankly speaking, out of the 400 million compatriots, half are men and half are women. Although both should work together to promote national products, the enthusiasm of women will certainly outweigh that of men. In recent years, foreign goods have increased daily, encompassing almost all four elements of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. They are cleverly designed, inexpensive, come in many categories, and offer a wide variety of styles, dazzling the eyes. The clothing that women themselves wear, as well as the clothing and food bought for their children, and the cosmetics used daily, make up a large portion of these goods. Moreover, the clothing worn by men and all the miscellaneous items in the home are mostly purchased by women. If all the women in the country can recognize that a strong neighbor is pressing in and that the country is facing a crisis, and from this year's National Products Year onward, make a major decision to avoid being seduced by the word "fashionable," regardless of the type of clothing, food, housing, and transportation items,

Promoting National Products Must Start with Women 216

— Ms. Baixue

"Women are the mothers of mankind, so promoting national products must start with women."

This is what my father said to me when I was reading the newspaper just now.

That's right, women are always the mothers of mankind, responsible for educating children, or, in a broader sense, responsible for educating mankind. Moreover, women are in charge of all household affairs, such as buying new clothes and miscellaneous items for the home. It is the women who propose what to buy and then hand it over to the men (or the women themselves or both men and women) to take care of it. Because men are almost always working outside, they don't pay much attention to household matters. Therefore, women are the most important people in the family.

Especially children, mothers must teach them to cultivate the habit of loving and using national products. To cultivate the habit of loving and using national products, first of all, there must be a good national product environment; to build this national product environment, all clothing, utensils, and equipment in the family must be completely national products.

If men want to buy foreign goods, women should dissuade them, and men will invariably listen. But if women want to buy foreign goods, men mostly go along with it; even if they try to dissuade them, it has very little effect. This is a shortcoming that women should eliminate.

Women, remember: Women are the mothers of mankind, promoting national products must start with women!

If we discard foreign goods and buy national products, then even if unscrupulous merchants seek huge profits and secretly sell inferior goods, because no one patronizes them, they will eventually switch to selling national products. Then, because national product factories have a wide sales market, they will inevitably strive for excellence, increase output, and lower prices. The commercial and socioeconomic situation of the country will inevitably develop gradually. Among the women in our country, those in Shanghai are the most fond of using imported goods, followed by those in cities, and then those in rural areas. The reason for this is indeed the harm caused by the word "fashionable." Shanghai is a diverse place with people from all over and a large number of foreign goods. The number of prostitutes is the highest in the country. Because of their business relationships, prostitutes compete to be the most unique and choose imported goods to decorate themselves, only seeking to be bright and eye-catching and to attract the attention of admirers, regardless of the outflow of profits and economic aggression. General mistresses and modern women admire their beauty and do not care about the source of money, and they follow suit, dressing flamboyantly and developing habits. Even young ladies from good families try their best to imitate them, and it is almost as if it is unfashionable not to use imported goods. In cities where this trend started early, it has become a common practice. Money flows out, day by day, and the sales of national products plummet. If the female compatriots in the intellectual class can lead by example, resist foreign goods, and switch to using national products, and everyone considers it shameful to use foreign goods and fashionable to use national products, it may not be impossible to change customs. I hope that Shanghai women will take advantage of this national crisis, actively proceed, and work together to be an example for the women of the country.

Me and National Products 217

— Pu Manbin

Checking things over. When my husband and I have free time, we often carefully check the clothing, food, housing, and personal belongings in our home and on our bodies to see if there are any non-national products. We often find that the thumbtacks and bookbinding staples used by the children do not have domestic products. One day, I accidentally saw this product at the Jiaotong University Exhibition and was very happy.

Parents set an example. Young children in the family are very imitative. They do as they see their parents do. Over the past few years, our family has gotten used to national products, and all the children like national products. Once, I gave Ah Wei a foreign cloth shirt that Ah Quan wore ten years ago. Ah Wei cried and said, "Father, mother, and brother all wear national clothes. Don't I love the country?" She finally took it off and was happy. One day, she was the vice mayor of the children's market at the China National Products Company. I put a new dress on her, and she secretly went to ask Mrs. Xu next door, "Is this a pure national product?" She was relieved when she got the answer.

Exchange conditions. Once, Mr. Xu Yangnan married off his daughter and invited Mr. Ren Zhi to be the wedding officiant. Mr. Ren Zhi said that if the new couple used national products, he would be happy to do so. This is also a good story in the Year of National Products. I advised my husband that he could use the same as an exchange condition in the future. Even entrusting someone to introduce a job, we must also set a rule that if you do not use national products, please do not patronize us.

Hate articles. During the Year of National Products, there were the most articles promoting national products. They were long and verbose, full of empty words, and really annoying. I said that instead of saying empty words, it is better to bury your head and actually do it. When I went back to my hometown to sweep the tombs this time, I met a person selling inferior cloth on the road. He was active in the countryside. My husband and I scolded him severely. Many villagers had some sense of right and wrong and said that this person specializes in selling Eastern cloth and should be scolded. As a result, the bastard ran away with his head in his hands. A very serious servant. One day, the servant bought three boxes of Swedish matches. I blamed her and insisted that she exchange them for national products. People said I was too serious. I said that if I let it go once, she would buy foreign goods again next time.

Understanding the Issue of Women Using National Products 218

— Jin Songtang

As the call to promote the use of national products is growing louder and louder, gentlemen in the national products industry are sparing no effort in their advocacy work, and they are indeed trying to make progress rapidly. However, upon closer examination of the understanding and use of national products by women in our country, it is still in its infancy. There are many reasons for this, which cannot be described in detail. Here, I offer my humble opinions to the national products production industry for consideration and improvement by those with greater wisdom:

"Insufficient intellect and lack of education." Our country's population is said to be 400 million, and of course, half of them are women. As everyone knows, according to the statistics of the Ministry of Education, more than 80% of the population has not received education, which means that only 20% of the people have received education. Moreover, China's long-standing habit of valuing men over women has not yet disappeared, so the number of women who have received considerable education is actually an absolute minority. During the period when the policy of dumping enemy goods was aggressively pursued, the market was filled with them, disguised and with many tricks. Even knowledgeable people are easily deceived by them, let alone women with a weak sense of awareness who only know that the value is low and cannot recognize these foreign goods behind masks? Therefore, the popularization of education should be the beginning of women's understanding of national products.

"Lack of common sense." Since their intellect is insufficient, their common sense is of course even more lacking. Women in our country have always valued etiquette and mostly stay at home, not knowing what society is like, let alone other things. In recent years, there have been calls for open socializing and advocating for women's occupations, but the number of unemployed men is everywhere, and the number of women with considerable jobs is just a drop in the ocean. Since they have little contact with society and rarely see or hear things, their common sense is naturally not broad. How can they not be fooled by foreign goods? Therefore, the simplicity and profundity of national product trademarks are also an aspect of women's identification and understanding.

"Strong spending power." In the current economic trend, which is becoming more and more turbulent, human consumption is becoming more and more extravagant. In addition, the influences of European and American culture are constantly being imported. The more civilized the material world, the more complicated life becomes. Taking Shanghai as an example, women's daily necessities and clothing, hats, socks, and shirts are constantly being renewed and changed, vying for novelty and beauty, and imported goods account for the majority. May I ask how much can be produced domestically? Although it is said that it is an expression of the vanity of the women's world,

A Virtuous Housewife 219

— Quan

The housewife is the head of the family, she is the main consumer of social economy, and at the same time, she is the owner of nurturing children and promoting future generations. Therefore, whether from a theoretical or practical point of view, a virtuous housewife should actively take on the responsibility of promoting national products.

Here is the story of Ms. Wang, a housewife worthy of being virtuous, promoting national products.

Before purchasing household items each time, Ms. Wang must discuss the budget with her husband. The first consideration is how to be the most economical, and the second is that she sincerely and kindly asks him to buy national products. Her husband is originally a patriotic young man with passion, and this further strengthens his determination to buy national products.

Every Sunday or public holiday, Ms. Wang's husband can get a chance to rest, and Ms. Wang takes her children to visit the National Products Exhibition Hall or to buy miscellaneous items at the National Products Company. In her opinion, this can prevent her husband from fooling around and wasting money elsewhere, and secondly, it can give the children some belief in using national products.

A relative, Mr. Li, is preparing to get married and sent an invitation. Ms. Wang then asked her husband to issue a gift certificate from the National Products Company to send it as a gift.

In fact, the patterns of domestic products are few and far between, lacking alternatives. In addition, the work and manufacturing are not exquisite enough to attract people. This is also a major obstacle in terms of understanding and use.

Since the opening of the China National Products Company, the public has gained a correct understanding, because domestic products are gathered in one place, making it convenient for purchasers, which is of no small significance. As a measure to popularize women's understanding, even a small trademark should be studied to make it simple and popular. Other aspects, such as the strangeness of the style, the exquisiteness of the work, and the low price, cater to the needs of the public and the psychology of women, are all of utmost importance.

From Her, Speaking of National Products 220

— Ms. Lu Weichi

Speaking of using national products, I can't help but recall her, whom I saw in Nanyang a few years ago. She was an Oriental woman, also residing in Annam, living next door to my house. The clothes she wore were, of course, made of goods from her own country. As for food, she mostly used canned goods produced in her own country. What baffled me most at first was that she would search for many wooden boxes in various cloth shops—wooden boxes used for packing Oriental cloth. It turned out she used them as firewood when cooking. Their family's daily necessities, even the smallest items, were all their own national products, not allowing any benefits to flow out. Their patriotism is truly worthy of admiration! The reason their country is so rich and strong is because their women and children have long recognized and resolved to choose national products. Alas! Speaking of our country, I am extremely ashamed! The conflicts between imperialist powers and their aggression against China are all for the purpose of seizing consumer markets to solve overproduction! China, alas, our Chinese people are still reveling in imported goods, and the erroneous concept of worshipping foreign goods has not yet been broken. If this continues, the future of Chinese national products will undoubtedly decline and fail. What hope is there for revitalization and expansion?

I believe that using national products is a virtue that citizens should possess, and promoting national products is a responsibility that citizens should bear. For the sake of national prosperity and strength, we cannot do without the movement to promote national products. The movement to promote national products should start with women, because women are the housewives in the family and have the power to choose all the daily necessities for the entire family. If Chinese women can emulate that Oriental woman, establishing a foundation of faith in national products, the future of national products can be expected to be bright. Not only that, but women occupy an important position in family education. They can usually do their best to promote the goodness of national products in front of children and how citizens should use national products, instilling in their young minds a good concept of loving and using national products, and planting a firm belief in national products. Dear sisters, since national products have such a close relationship with us, then we should quickly rise up, shoulder our important mission, engage in the movement to promote national products, and do our best to promote the glory of China and develop the outlet for national products. (March 31st, at the female dormitory of Jinan University.)

A True Account of the National Products Movement in Shanghai Women's Circles 221

— Qia Cheng

The twenty-second year of the Republic of China is considered the year of national products. In this year, we must establish the reputation of national products and, more importantly, confirm our belief in national products, hoping to spread it from cities to villages and complete this important mission. In this great national products movement, it just so happens that our National Products Weekly was born, so we are even more excited to shout.

This self-proclaimed power cannot be complacent, but the Shanghai women's national products movement was inspired by Mr. Yang Yan's "The Responsibilities of Housewives." Because the fact is so, we cannot deny it.
